\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ For\ now,\ \_interpreter\ is\ implemented\ as\ a\ singleton\ since\ its\ currently\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ possible\ to\ have\ multiple\ independent\ embedded\ python\ interpreters\ without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ patching\ the\ python\ source\ code\ or\ starting\ a\ separate\ process\ for\ each.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ [1]\ Furthermore,\ many\ python\ objects\ expect\ that\ they\ are\ destructed\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ same\ thread\ as\ they\ were\ constructed.\ [2]\ So\ for\ advanced\ usage,\ a\ \`{}kill()`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ function\ is\ provided\ so\ that\ library\ users\ can\ manually\ ensure\ that\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ interpreter\ is\ constructed\ and\ destroyed\ within\ the\ same\ thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
